Yet as the root descends, the branches also diverge,
and falsehoods masquerade as truth while the proper becomes distorted.
The heart of chastity and integrity gradually declines,
and the steadfastness of the pine and cypress is rarely seen.
Great principles remain obscured,
and who recognizes the mysterious workings?

Though the Three Teachings offer awakening words,
through the ages few have specialized in this discourse.
To rouse and admonish—
this is my compassion;
to proclaim and propagate—
this is your duty.

According to the memorial requesting the exposition of the *Nü Jing*’s alchemical principles,
the sentiments and words were earnest and sincere,
sharing the same salvific intent.
The details were thorough,
rooted in the sincere quest for the hidden truth of the Red Dragon,
opening a bridge for the Way of women.

The tally matched,
initiating instruction for the unenlightened among women.
At an opportune time, it was to be disseminated,
and promptly forwarded for deliberation.
After consultation,
the transcendent script was inscribed,
a karmic affinity from past lives,
using this to awaken the common folk.
The Left Bureau planted the immortal bones
from former existences,
relying on this to propagate the great transformation,
undertaking this monumental task,
assisting Heaven’s work.

The Original Lady was commanded to select an auspicious day for expounding the scripture,
and the host of perfected ones were ordered to enact the teachings in due time.
The words were drawn from sincerity,
awakening the delusions of the world’s inner chambers;
the text was refined and pure,
establishing a model of maternal virtue for later generations.

The excellence of these fourteen chapters, perfected through countless kalpas of transcendence, is now specially decreed for dissemination—let this command be reverently received and never neglected.

From the *Recorded Sayings of Heavenly Lord Wang*:
Previously, upon Jin Zi’s memorial petitioning the Original Lady to determine whether the female disciple Lin Ying was suitable for instruction in cultivation, and whether those permitted to expound the scripture were appropriate, an imperial decree was issued ordering the local City God’s Bureau to examine Lin Ying’s karmic records from past and present lives and submit a memorial to the Imperial Lord. Now, according to the memorial received, it is found that Lin Ying’s past three lives originated as a scholar of the Ming dynasty’s Chenghua era in Weiyang, surnamed Wei, named Wenxi. Though upright in conduct and never entering officialdom, he indulged in ostentatious eloquence, weaving ornate falsehoods, mocking his peers, and disparaging esteemed predecessors. Moreover, he violated the precept against lust, and thus was punished in his second life by rebirth as a woman, placed in the monastic order to endure hardship. At that time, during the Tianqi era’s middle years, she was reborn in Wu, in the western village of Kunlun Mountain County, to the Cao family—this being her third life. Due to her vow of purity, during her monastic existence she maintained a resolute will, practicing austerities and revering the Most High. She encountered the female Dharma-teacher Dinghui of Zhongshan, who instructed her in the cultivation of mysterious arts and the contemplation of the Great Yin’s alchemical techniques for refining form. Regrettably, before mastering them, she lightly abandoned the world. That she now receives this karmic affinity is indeed rooted in the seeds sown three lives prior.

Further investigation reveals that though she is now a woman and still young, she bears no grave transgressions. The reason she suffers the retribution of a female rebirth is that the sin of ornate falsehood remains unresolved. All these details were memorialized and reported.

Additionally, according to the memorial from the Dharma-hall Inspector, Chunxiu is currently engaged in the Rite of the Dipper to beseech blessings and repent sins. The Original Lady is greatly pleased and has petitioned the Imperial Lord to bestow further transformation and deliverance. Once the Rite of the Dipper is complete, she is to submit a formal memorial to repent sins and seek grace. The Original Lady will select an auspicious time to descend and personally instruct her, awaiting the scripture’s exposition.

By the command of the Imperial Lord and the Original Lady, Jin Benzun, as Chunxiu’s preceptor in transmission, is to be questioned whether he can guarantee her unwavering devotion to the end. A clear memorial is to be submitted in response.

Though this karmic cause appears remote, by the Imperial Lord’s decree, the planchette’s sand is specially employed to reveal it: the retribution for ornate falsehood persists even after two lifetimes as a woman. Now, by virtue of her monastic cultivation in a past life, she has entered the Dharma assembly. If she can transmit the alchemical teachings with sincere and unshakable devotion, her past defilements will be entirely purified, and her immortal affinity may be fulfilled.

Let Chunxiu take heed of this! Be solemn!

The *Recorded Discourses of Lady Wanyun*

By the Imperial Lord’s decree of pardon, I have reviewed the memorial submitted by Jin Benzun, which states that the devout woman of refining brushwork, Lin Chunxiu, has firmly resolved to advance in cultivation with unwavering sincerity, her wisdom-nature clear and keen, making her fit for the office of transmission. Her petition, both in its earlier and later submissions, has been fully reported to the commanding generals for response. Now, I am specially commanded to personally instruct her at the altar of our Lin lineage, guiding her to lucid awakening. Once her brush attains penetrating insight, she may serve as my proxy in expounding the subtleties of the Dao.

Heaven and Earth, yin and yang, take different forms yet function in mutual dependence. The male, modeled on *qian*, embodies firmness and strength, his form established in vigor, his *qi* received as purity. The female, modeled on *kun*, embodies steadfastness and softness, her form established in yielding, her *qi* received as turbidity. Purity is light, turbidity is heavy; the light and pure image Heaven, the heavy and turbid image Earth. Yet Heaven, though yang, contains yin within—embodying Earth’s response above; Earth, though yin, contains yang within—embodying Heaven’s union below. Thus the Two Modes arise from the Supreme Ultimate, and yin and yang reside in male and female.

Know this: Heaven’s body is non-action, pure emptiness, lofty and distant. Though it steams clouds and rains moisture to nourish the earth below, it cannot itself gestate, nurture, or sustain the ten thousand beings. Therefore, for men, the work of cultivating the Real is arduous. As for women, likened to Earth—though they bear mountains and receive rivers, congealing in thickness and weight—yet the hundred grasses and myriad things sprout in due season. By reversing the usual course, they may raise yang *qi* at the Spring Equinox and emit harmonious radiance at the Winter Solstice. This is analogous to the mechanism of female gestation, sharing in the same ceaseless generative wonder. Thus, for women, the cultivation of the Real is far simpler than for men.

In sum, the worldly are beset by desires, and so they distance themselves from the Dao. The perfected are free of desire, and so they attain the Dao. Regardless of gender, those who know that reducing desire leads to the Dao may enter it. For without desire, one is pure; pure, one is still; still, one is luminous; luminous, one abides in profound tranquility and constant reality, the thusness of the original body, universally aware and illumined. The pearl of wisdom-nature in the ocean of consciousness shines forth—how could this be merely a marvel wrought at the tip of a brush?

I pity the women of the world, who deem themselves base and defiled, sunk in delusion and degradation. For many years, I have wished to expound the alchemical scriptures to deliver them from suffering, and have spoken of this often with Jin Benzun. Now, Lin Chunxiu’s karmic roots are keen, and to have attained a human rebirth three times is already rare. Though she bears past defilements, they may be repented and cleansed. Having now received this instruction, she should diligently engage in contemplative study, purify her heart, reduce desires, and devote herself with utmost sincerity. Not only may she then propagate my esoteric texts for the salvation of the world, but she may also enjoy blessings, bear worthy descendants, and, having fulfilled this karmic female form, follow me in carefree wandering through the celestial palaces.

Strive on! Be solemn!
